Welcome to

Social Food Hallon Main

Three chef-driven eateries, craft cocktails, duckpin bowling, and a place that feels like home — right in the heart of downtown Elizabethtown, KY.

⭐ 4.5 Google Stars

Our Story

More Than a
Food Hall

Social is a community gathering place where flavor, creativity, and connection come together. Housed in a beautifully restored historic building in the heart of downtown, we bring together multiple chef-driven food concepts under one welcoming roof.

Whether you're grabbing a quick lunch, celebrating with the family, or settling in for a long evening with great cocktails and duckpin bowling — Social is where Elizabethtown comes together.

Eat at Social

Our Eateries

Three distinct kitchens, one incredible space. Find something for everyone.

🍕

Maillard Wood Fired Kitchen

A wood fired kitchen specializing in Neo-Neapolitan pizza and other wood fired fare, while also offering custom menus for catered events.

View Menu
🍣

Wasabi Bistro

Whether you're craving delicate sushi rolls or a rich, steaming bowl of ramen, every bite is made to order with authenticity and passion.

View Menu
🍔

StrEAT Kitchen

Our newest vendor is serving up smash burgers, loaded hot dogs, sweet redemptions, and bold flavors that make it easy to feed your whole crew.

View More

What's Inside

Play Together

🍴

Three Eateries

Multiple chef-driven food concepts in one space, so everyone at the table can get exactly what they're craving.

Chef-Driven
🎳

Duckpin Bowling

A classic, smaller-ball variation of bowling that's perfect for all ages and skill levels. Book a lane while you dine!

Family Fun
🍺

Beer Taps

A rotating lineup of draft beers on tap — local favorites, craft picks, and classics. Something cold for everyone.

Craft Selections
🍸

Cocktails & Wine

Cocktail spouts, curated wine selections, and skilled bartenders who are always the sweetest. Your perfect drink awaits.

Great Cocktails
🐕

Dog-Friendly Patio

Bring the whole family — pups included! Our outdoor patio welcomes your four-legged friends on any beautiful day.

Pets Welcome

Meet the Maker

The Vision
Behind Social

Social on Main didn't happen by accident. It took one person with a bold idea, a deep love for Elizabethtown, and a belief that this community deserved a gathering place as warm and vibrant as the people who call it home.

From hand-picking each chef-driven vendor to designing a space where families, friends, and neighbors could come together — every detail of Social reflects a personal commitment to community, creativity, and connection.

"

Good vibes. Good friends.
You lucky people.
